if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'abcae7c7601397f9201e393037a2787d0902051b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'abcae7c7601397f9201e393037a2787d0902051b') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'f0792f70df7e126d5f52ef9e17fa4205d0bc03b7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'abcae7c7601397f9201e393037a2787d0902051b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/uuid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== '400c6f810b04b7a42972d689db39b6c4b5e6c56c') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== 'e1b5a4a4ff97f1fe178c377c5c2f2d555b733e4e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/uuid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

			if (!@copy('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/uuid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== '400c6f810b04b7a42972d689db39b6c4b5e6c56c') {

		}

if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1248') err('Could not write to .version.php!');
